# Grafana Configuration File Parsing and Override Chain

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in grafana/grafana that implement configuration loading: the INI file parser, the environment variable override logic, the default values per section, and the sensitive config value masking for the /api/admin/settings endpoint.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the platform domain.

    29→func (hs *HTTPServer) AdminGetSettings(c *contextmodel.ReqContext) response.Response {
    30→	settings, err := hs.getAuthorizedSettings(c.Req.Context(), c.SignedInUser, hs.SettingsProvider.Current())
    31→	if err != nil {
    32→		return response.Error(http.StatusForbidden, "Failed to authorize settings", err)
    33→	}
    34→	return response.JSON(http.StatusOK, settings)
    35→}

    14→
    15→type ValidationError struct {
    16→	Errors []error
    17→}
    18→
    19→func (v ValidationError) Error() string {
    20→	builder := strings.Builder{}
    21→
    22→	for i, e := range v.Errors {
    23→		builder.WriteString(e.Error())
    24→		if i != len(v.Errors)-1 {
    25→			builder.WriteString(", ")
    26→		}
    27→	}
    28→
    29→	return builder.String()
    30→}
    31→
    32→// Provider is a settings provider abstraction

    36→type Provider interface {
    37→	// Current returns a SettingsBag with a static copy of
    38→	// the current configured pairs of key/values for each
    39→	// configuration section.

    41→
    42→	CurrentVerbose() VerboseSettingsBag
    43→
    44→	// Update receives a SettingsBag with the pairs of key/values
    45→	// to be updated per section and a SettingsRemovals with the
    46→	// section keys to be removed.
    47→	Update(updates SettingsBag, removals SettingsRemovals) error
    48→	// KeyValue returns a key-value abstraction
    49→	// for the given pair of section and key.
    50→	KeyValue(section, key string) KeyValue
    51→	// Section returns a settings section

   963→func (cfg *Cfg) loadConfiguration(args CommandLineArgs) (*ini.File, error) {
   964→	// load config defaults
   965→	defaultConfigFile := path.Join(cfg.HomePath, "conf/defaults.ini")
   966→	cfg.configFiles = append(cfg.configFiles, defaultConfigFile)
   967→
   968→	// check if config file exists
   969→	if _, err := os.Stat(defaultConfigFile); os.IsNotExist(err) {
   970→		fmt.Println("Grafana-server Init Failed: Could not find config defaults, make sure homepath command line parameter is set or working directory is homepath")
   971→		os.Exit(1)
   972→	}
   973→
   974→	// load defaults
   975→	parsedFile, err := ini.Load(defaultConfigFile)
   976→	if err != nil {
   977→		fmt.Printf("Failed to parse defaults.ini, %v\n", err)
   978→		os.Exit(1)
   979→		return nil, err
   980→	}
   981→
   982→	// command line props
   983→	commandLineProps := cfg.getCommandLineProperties(args.Args)
   984→	// load default overrides
   985→	cfg.applyCommandLineDefaultProperties(commandLineProps, parsedFile)
   986→

   988→	err = cfg.loadSpecifiedConfigFile(args.Config, parsedFile)
   989→	if err != nil {
   990→		err2 := cfg.initLogging(parsedFile)
   991→		if err2 != nil {
   992→			return nil, err2
   993→		}
   994→		cfg.Logger.Error(err.Error())
   995→		os.Exit(1)
   996→	}
   997→
   998→	// apply environment overrides
   999→	err = cfg.applyEnvVariableOverrides(parsedFile)
  1000→	if err != nil {
  1001→		return nil, err
  1002→	}
  1003→
  1004→	// apply command line overrides
  1005→	cfg.applyCommandLineProperties(commandLineProps, parsedFile)
  1006→
  1007→	// evaluate config values containing environment variables
  1008→	err = expandConfig(parsedFile)
  1009→	if err != nil {
  1010→		return nil, err
  1011→	}

   660→func RedactedValue(key, value string) string {
   661→	if value == "" {
   662→		return ""
   663→	}
   664→
   665→	uppercased := strings.ToUpper(key)
   666→	// Sensitive information: password, secrets etc
   667→	for _, pattern := range []string{
   668→		"PASSWORD",
   669→		"SECRET",
   670→		"PROVIDER_CONFIG",
   671→		"PRIVATE_KEY",
   672→		"SECRET_KEY",
   673→		"CERTIFICATE",
   674→		"ACCOUNT_KEY",
   675→		"ENCRYPTION_KEY",
   676→		"VAULT_TOKEN",
   677→		"CLIENT_SECRET",
   678→		"ENTERPRISE_LICENSE",
   679→		"API_DB_PASS",
   680→		"^TOKEN$",
   681→		"ID_FORWARDING_TOKEN$",
   682→		"AUTHENTICATION_TOKEN$",
   683→		"AUTH_TOKEN$",
   684→		"RENDERER_TOKEN$",
   685→		"API_TOKEN$",
   686→		"WEBHOOK_TOKEN$",
   687→		"INSTALL_TOKEN$",
   688→	} {
   689→		if match, err := regexp.MatchString(pattern, uppercased); match && err == nil {
   690→			return RedactedPassword
   691→		}
   692→	}
   693→
   694→	for _, exception := range []string{
   695→		"RUDDERSTACK",
   696→		"APPLICATION_INSIGHTS",
   697→		"SENTRY",
   698→	} {
   699→		if strings.Contains(uppercased, exception) {
   700→			return value
   701→		}
   702→	}
   703→
   704→	if u, err := RedactedURL(value); err == nil {
   705→		return u
   706→	}
   707→
   708→	return value
   709→}
   710→
   711→func RedactedURL(value string) (string, error) {
   712→	// Value could be a list of URLs
   713→	chunks := util.SplitString(value)
   714→
   715→	for i, chunk := range chunks {
   716→		var hasTmpPrefix bool
   717→		const tmpPrefix = "http://"
   718→
   719→		if !strings.Contains(chunk, "://") {
   720→			chunk = tmpPrefix + chunk
   721→			hasTmpPrefix = true
   722→		}
   723→
   724→		u, err := url.Parse(chunk)
   725→		if err != nil {
   726→			return "", err
   727→		}
   728→

   855→func EnvKey(sectionName string, keyName string) string {
   856→	sN := strings.ToUpper(strings.ReplaceAll(sectionName, ".", "_"))
   857→	sN = strings.ReplaceAll(sN, "-", "_")
   858→	kN := strings.ToUpper(strings.ReplaceAll(keyName, ".", "_"))
   859→	envKey := fmt.Sprintf("GF_%s_%s", sN, kN)
   860→	return envKey
   861→}

   863→func (cfg *Cfg) applyCommandLineDefaultProperties(props map[string]string, file *ini.File) {
   864→	cfg.appliedCommandLineProperties = make([]string, 0)
   865→	for _, section := range file.Sections() {
   866→		for _, key := range section.Keys() {
   867→			keyString := fmt.Sprintf("default.%s.%s", section.Name(), key.Name())
   868→			value, exists := props[keyString]
   869→			if exists {
   870→				key.SetValue(value)
   871→				cfg.appliedCommandLineProperties = append(cfg.appliedCommandLineProperties,
   872→					fmt.Sprintf("%s=%s", keyString, RedactedValue(keyString, value)))
   873→			}
   874→		}
   875→	}
   876→}
   877→
   878→func (cfg *Cfg) applyCommandLineProperties(props map[string]string, file *ini.File) {
   879→	for _, section := range file.Sections() {
   880→		sectionName := section.Name() + "."
   881→		if section.Name() == ini.DefaultSection {
   882→			sectionName = ""
   883→		}
   884→		for _, key := range section.Keys() {
   885→			keyString := sectionName + key.Name()
   886→			value, exists := props[keyString]
   887→			if exists {
   888→				cfg.appliedCommandLineProperties = append(cfg.appliedCommandLineProperties, fmt.Sprintf("%s=%s", keyString, value))
   889→				key.SetValue(value)
   890→			}
   891→		}
   892→	}
   893→}

    14→
    15→type ValidationError struct {
    16→	Errors []error
    17→}
    18→
    19→func (v ValidationError) Error() string {
    20→	builder := strings.Builder{}
    21→
    22→	for i, e := range v.Errors {
    23→		builder.WriteString(e.Error())
    24→		if i != len(v.Errors)-1 {
    25→			builder.WriteString(", ")
    26→		}
    27→	}
    28→
    29→	return builder.String()
    30→}

func RedactedValue(key, value string) string {
	if value == "" {
		return ""
	}

	uppercased := strings.ToUpper(key)
	// Sensitive information: password, secrets etc
	for _, pattern := range []string{
		"PASSWORD",
		"SECRET",
		"PROVIDER_CONFIG",
--
func EnvKey(sectionName string, keyName string) string {
	sN := strings.ToUpper(strings.ReplaceAll(sectionName, ".", "_"))
	sN = strings.ReplaceAll(sN, "-", "_")
	kN := strings.ToUpper(strings.ReplaceAll(keyName, ".", "_"))
	envKey := fmt.Sprintf("GF_%s_%s", sN, kN)
	return envKey
}

### Core Configuration Files (pkg/setting/)

These files handle the main INI configuration parsing, environment variable overrides, and default values:

1. **pkg/setting/setting.go** - Main configuration file with:
   - `NewCfg()` - Creates new configuration
   - `NewCfgFromBytes()` - Creates config from INI bytes
   - `NewCfgFromINIFile()` - Creates config from ini.File
   - `NewCfgFromBytesWithoutJSValidation()` - Alternative constructor
   - `NewCfgFromArgs()` - Creates config from command line args
   - `loadConfiguration()` - Loads INI configuration files
   - `applyEnvVariableOverrides()` - Applies GF_* environment overrides
   - `EnvKey()` - Generates GF_SECTION_KEY environment variable names
   - `RedactedValue()` - Redacts/masks sensitive values like passwords and secrets
   - Contains `Cfg` struct with `Raw *ini.File` field

2. **pkg/setting/provider.go** - Settings provider abstraction:
   - `Provider` interface - Settings provider with thread-safety
   - `OSSImpl` - Open source implementation
   - `Current()` - Returns current settings with redaction applied
   - `CurrentVerbose()` - Returns verbose settings with source tracking
   - `SettingsBag` and `VerboseSettingsBag` types
   - Implements redaction using `RedactedValue()` function

3. **pkg/setting/expanders.go** - Configuration expansion/templating:
   - `Expander` interface - Generic expander interface
   - `expandConfig()` - Expands config variables
   - `envExpander` - Expands environment variab

## Summary of Grafana Configuration Loading Implementation

### **Key Files Found (32 total)**

**Core Configuration Files (pkg/setting/)**

- `provider.go` - Settings provider abstraction with thread-safe access
- `expanders.go` - Configuration variable expansion (env variables, file contents)
- 26 setting_*.go files for section-specific configuration

**API & Infrastructure**
- `pkg/api/admin.go` - `/api/admin/settings` endpoint implementation
- `pkg/configprovider/configprovider.go` - Configuration abstraction layer
- `pkg/infra/log/log.go` - Logging configuration

### **Key Symbols Identified (35 total)**

**Configuration Loading Chain:**
1. `NewCfgFromArgs()` → `Load()` → `loadConfiguration()`
2. Apply overrides: command-line defaults, env vars, command-line args
3. `expandConfig()` - expand variables in config values
4. `parseINIFile()` - parse INI structure into Cfg
5. `ProvideProvider()` → `Current()` - create settings provider with redaction

**Environment Variable Overrides:**
- `applyEnvVariableOverrides()` applies `GF_SECTION_KEY` pattern overrides
- `EnvKey()` converts section.key to GF_SECTION_KEY format

**Sensitive Value Masking:**
- `RedactedValue()` masks passwords, secrets, tokens, keys
- `RedactedURL()` redacts URLs with credentials
- Applied automatically in `OSSImpl.Current()` method

**Admin API:**
- `AdminGetSettings()` - GET `/api/admin/settings`
- `getAuthorizedSettings()` - filters by user permissions

It supports environment variable expansion via envExpander and file content expansion via fileExpander, using a regex pattern to identify expandable values marked with $(VARIABLE) or $__file(FILEPATH) syntax.\\n\\n**Sensitive Value Masking**: The RedactedValue() function in pkg/setting/setting.go (line 660) implements the masking/redaction logic. It identifies sensitive configuration keys by pattern matching against keywords like PASSWORD, SECRET, PROVIDER_CONFIG, PRIVATE_KEY, SECRET_KEY, CERTIFICATE, ACCOUNT_KEY, ENCRYPTION_KEY, VAULT_TOKEN, CLIENT_SECRET, ENTERPRISE_LICENSE, API_DB_PASS, and various *TOKEN patterns. When matched, these values are replaced with the RedactedPassword constant (***********). URLs are also redacted using the RedactedURL() function. Exceptions are made for certain trusted services like RUDDERSTACK, APPLICATION_INSIGHTS, and SENTRY.\\n\\n**Settings Provider Implementation**: The Provider interface in pkg/setting/provider.go (line 36) defines the abstraction for accessing configuration. The OSSImpl type implements this interface, with methods:\\n- Current() returns a SettingsBag (nested map of strings) with all current settings, applying RedactedValue() to sensitive keys\\n- CurrentVerbose() returns a VerboseSettingsBag with source tracking (DB vs System)\\n- Update() and RegisterReloadHandler() support dynamic configuration updates\\n\\n**Section-Specific Configuration**: The setting_*.go files in pkg/setting/ contain functions that parse INI sections for specific features (auth, plugins, alerting, SMTP, etc.). Each module reads its configuration section from the INI file and populates typed fields in the Cfg struct using methods like MustString(), MustBool(), MustInt(), and MustDuration().\\n\\n**Admin Settings API**: The /api/admin/settings endpoint is implemented in pkg/api/admin.go. The AdminGetSettings() function (line 29) retrieves current settings using hs.SettingsProvider.Current() and filters results based on user permissions via getAuthorizedSettings(). The getAuthorizedSettings() function checks access control permissions (ac.ActionSettingsRead) for settings:* scopes and returns only authorized settings. Similarly, AdminGetVerboseSettings() provides detailed settings with source information.\\n\\n**Configuration Provider Abstraction**: The ConfigProvider interface in pkg/configprovider/configprovider.go provides a high-level abstraction for configuration access, used by other services to access configuration values without direct dependency on the setting package.\\n\\nThe entire system is designed to support a clear override chain: defaults.ini \u2192 custom INI files \u2192 environment variables (GF_*) \u2192 command-line arguments, with sensitive values masked at the API boundary to prevent exposing secrets to users. The SettingsBag types and Provider interface enable thread-safe access to configuration and support future runtime updates to configuration values.\"\n}\n",
